aRwerilobiTi nawili:


v. S-Svilma sarCeliT mimarTa sasamarTlos da miuTiTa, rom 1999


wlis 17 ivniss q. TbilisSi meliqiSvilis moedanze gaCerebul taqss `mi-


cubiSi lanseri~ ukana mxridan daejaxa avtomanqana `mersedesi~, ro-


melsac marTavda TurqeTis moqalaqe i. m-iTi. SejaxebiT gamowveuli


inerciiT misi manqana Tavis mxriv daejaxa win mdgom Jiguls, romelsac


marTavda moqalaqe z. g-Ze.


mosarCele aRniSnavda, rom avtoavariis Sedegad iqve myofma avto-


inspeqciis TanamSromlebma Seadgines oqmi, romlis mixedviTac erT-


erT damrRvevad TviT is cnes, rac ar Seefereba sinamdviles.


mosarCele moiTxovda sagzao policiis mier Sedgenili oqmis gauq-


mebas da mopasuxisagan misi braliT dazianebuli avtomanqanebis aRdge-


nas. igi miuTiTebda, rom misi avtomanqanis aRdgenis Rirebuleba Sead-


gens 1617 lars, xolo z. g-Zis 300 lars. aseve moiTxovda mocdenis Sede-


gad gaSvebul mogebas da saijaro gadasaxads.


mopasuxem sarCeli ar cno. misi ganmartebiT manqana, romelic mis win


midioda meore manqanas daejaxa da inerciiT ukan daixia, ris Sedegadac


maTi manqanebi msubuqad Seejaxnen erTmaneTs.


isani-samgoris raionuli sasamarTlos 2000 wlis 28 ivlisis gadaw-


yvetilebiT sarCeli dakmayofilda nawilobriv. mopasuxes mosarCelis


sasargeblod daekisra 1804 laris da 572 aSS dolaris eqvivalenti


erovnuli valutiT.


Tbilisis saolqo sasamarTlos 2000 wlis 7 noembris ganCinebiT i. m-


iTis saapelacio saCivari ar dakmayofilda.


saapelacio palatam daadgina, rom mopasuxem gaufrTxilebeli moq-


medebiT daarRvia sagzao moZraobis wesebi, rasac Sedegad mohyva gaCere-


bul avtomanqanaze Sejaxeba, ris Sedegadac S-Svils miadga ziani. saape-


lacio palatam aseve dadgenilad miaCnia, rom S-Svils sagzao moZraobis


wesebi ar daurRvevia, ris gamoc mas brali ar miuZRvis zianis dadgomaSi.
